< Review>
I would normally give KFC a two star rating for their mediocre chicken and their horrible sides.  What brought it down to a one start is their chicken wings.  We thought we'd give them a try one day.  What a mistake.  Absolutely the worst wings I've ever had in my life.  We ended up throwing them out.  The coatings are more than the chicken, the meat is dry and old, and they actually include the wing tips, which are inedible.  KFC has gone way down in quality overall, but this experience has turned me away from ever going back.  I'm now on my search for a descent fried chicken place near me.< /Review>

This place is mediocre at best. It seems everyone wants a speedy service. I prefer to have them take a minute to prep the area.
I found prepping the area with baby powder as well as applying a soothing gel post-threading is beneficial. I don't have sensitive skin but broke out in small bumps.
I also have never had to request for the finishing touch- the scissor trim on the beginning area of my eyebrows. Here, I had too.
Overall, the shape of my eyebrows were fairly done. Two stars because prepping the area is half the service.<//text>

<Text>I found CarSight through a post that Michael made on Facebook. He was very responsive, answered my questions, and got me a carfax so I could review the maintenance on the Subaru Outback I was interested in. I set up a time to come to the lot and when I got there the car was pulled out and ready for a test drive.

Michael handed me the keys and told me to take it for a drive and take my time looking the vehicle over. Since he knew I had done my research and knew quite a bit about this make/model he didn't hover as I evaluated the vehicle.

I took my time and then came in to discuss pricing. They have a really nice and unique system that makes it easy to see and understand the pricing on the vehicle, the dmv fees, taxes etc. We looked it over and then discussed the pricing. It was no pressure and I paid a price I was satisfied with.

Could I have gotten a better deal? I'm not entirely sure. What I do know is that it was the most painless buying experience I've ever had and my interactions with Michael didn't give me anxiety like a typical dealership would.
